 guru poornima (guru Purnima) kaa hindu dharm main vishesh mahatv he
 Among Hindus, Guru has the best position
 yahaan tak ki guru kaa darja bhagwaan se bhi upar he kyonki wo guru hi he jo hamen agyanta ke andhkaar se ubarkar sahi maarg kii ore le jaataa he
 This is the reason that Guru Purnima is celebrated with great pomp across the country
 manyata he ki isi din aadiguru, mahabharat ke rachayita or chaar vedon ke vyaakhyaata maharishi krishna dwaipayan vyas yani ki maharishi veda vyas (ved Vyas) kaa janm hua tha
 He was a great Sanskrit scholar
 mahabharat (mahabharat) jaisaa mahakavy unheen kii dein he
 In the 18th chapter of this, Lord Shri Krishna teaches the Gita
 sabhi 18 puraanon kaa rachayita bhi maharishi vedavyas ko mana jaataa he
 He is also credited with dividing the Vedas
 isi kaaran inkaa naam vedavyas padaa tha

 sawaal 1
 Is the Aadhaar card still valid? Answer - The Supreme Court has said that the Aadhaar card is constitutional, but it cannot be made compulsory anywhere

 sawaal 3
 Will private companies have to provide Aadhaar information? Answer - Private companies cannot do their own arbitrariness on Aadhaar card
 supreme court ne aadhaar act ke dhara 57 ko khatm kar diya he

 sawaal 4
 Will the children be admissible for admission to the school? Answer - The Supreme Court has clearly stated in its judgment that schools cannot demand Aadhaar card for the admission of children of 6 to 14 years
 isse pehle skool bacchon kaa bhi aadhaar card maangate the

 Aadhaar card is completely safe
 sawaal 6
 Is Aadhaar card necessary for examinations? Answer - CBSE, NEET, UGC can no longer make Aadhaar card mandatory for any exam
 sawaal 7
 Will Aadhaar card be required to file income tax? Answer - The Supreme Court has removed the requirement of Aadhaar from bank accounts - mobile, but Aadhaar card is still necessary for filing income tax returns
 sawaal 8
 Is Aadhaar still necessary for PAN card? Answer - If you want to get PAN card, then Aadhaar card is mandatory for that
 sawaal 9
 Is Aadhaar card necessary for availing government schemes? Answer - If you have to take advantage of government schemes then it is necessary to have an Aadhar card
 sawaal 10
 Is the common man's data safe in Aadhaar? Answer - Aadhaar card is safe, but the Supreme Court has ordered the government to enact laws to protect the data in the Aadhaar card at the earliest

 Gandhi's idea of non-violence was based on the practice of Satyagraha, in which the other is replaced by his own suffering
 ise unhone 'aatma kii cheer-faad' kaha tha
